                      <div data-reactid="413">
                       Stay with us at one of the most beautiful country clubs in the Coachella Valley! Our lovely tennis villa is on the Palmer golf course and located in the middle of Mission Hills Country Club! We are also open to HomeSwaps anywhere in the world! Message us!
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="414">
                       Our home is located at the prestigious Mission Hills Country Club in the heart of Rancho Mirage. Our two bedroom tennis villa has two spacious master bedrooms (each with a luxurious king or California king sized bed), 2 bathrooms, flat-screen TVs in each room and super fast wifi! Our home has a warm, modern feel with full furnishings, vaulted ceilings, patio, rooftop deck and most of the home has been recently renovated. World-class golf courses are just minutes away as well as public tennis courts, hiking trails and The Living Desert Zoo. We are about 15 minutes from the Indian Wells Tennis Gardens, El Paseo Drive, The River, various restaurants, wine bars, and tons of shopping - even Downtown Palm Springs! The Westin Mission Hills is right next door which is usually a shuttle stop for Coachella and Desert Trip. Restrictions: - Nightly rates are for 4 guests maximum - Children are welcome but our home is not child proof nor do we offer anything specifically for children unfortunately. - Security deposit is $300 due upon reservation and will be refunded upon check out pending inspection (taken through AirBnB) - Cleaning fee of $125 - Any group staying longer than two weeks will have a required second cleaning fee during their stay. This is to help maintain the home and to ensure you enjoy your stay. - No pets - No smoking - No events Other Things to Note: - We are in a gated Country Club so you will get access through the main gate. - We are NOT members of the tennis club or golf club here at Mission Hills, so you will not have access to the tennis courts or golf courses during your stay (unless you know a member). - You will not have garage parking but there are plenty of parking spaces right outside of our home. HomeSwaps: If you are interesting in swapping homes, we are totally open to it! We are interested in traveling anywhere, so please feel free to ask! As long as you have an Airbnb listed that is relatively comparable we would be happy to consider it. Thanks! :)
                      </div>

                     <div data-reactid="1022">
                      <div data-reactid="1023">
                       Brand new luxurious private estate in prime Rancho Mirage location. This newly built 4350 sq ft modern gem is set on approx. 1/2 acre of private property with stunning mountain views, along with your infinity pool &amp; spa. Close to restaurants, grocery, parks, and art &amp; culture. You’ll love the high ceilings, top of the line furnishings &amp; appliances, views, location, and much more. Desert Anna is great place for couples to unwind in the desert with every luxury imaginable at your fingertips.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1024">
                       Brand new architectural home.&nbsp; The most expansive and private residence at the newly completed Vail Dunes development in Rancho Mirage.&nbsp; Featuring 4350 sq. ft. of modern living space, 10-14' Ceilings, 3 Bedrooms including a casita with separate entrance, 4 baths, home gym, media room, Master Suite Retreat with His &amp; Hers vanities, Soaking Tub, Steam Shower with dual rain showers, walk-in closet and 3 Car Garage. High-end finish details include 24x24 designer tiled flooring in main living areas, smooth finish drywall, solid quartz &amp; stone counter tops and custom cabinetry walnut millwork throughout. Fixture package features the brand names of Miele (full size oven, steam oven, built-in coffee) Thermador (gourmet fridge and Freedom induction cooktop), Hans Grohe, Kohler and Designer Lighting from Bocce. This home was made for entertaining in high-style and enjoying the year-round sunshine that Rancho Mirage is known for. Discover thoughtful designer appointments around every corner, inside and out, of this beautiful vacation home. SMART HOME is powered by an RTI custom home automation processor that controls the homes lighting, automated blinds, TV’s, music, fireplace, pool &amp; spa, misters, security alarm, and even the garage door. Several custom ‘scenes’ are preprogrammed to help set the mood at a touch of a button which adjusts multiple items. The system is controlled by the iPad which is provided for use, and via several RTI remote controls and in-wall touchscreens throughout the house. Do not worry if you are not good with this type of thing – it was designed with ease of use in mind and so that visitors could easily use the controls. THE KITCHEN - is bright and has everything you need for preparing gourmet meals and hosting friends and family. This kitchen features double Miele ovens (one is also a steam/convection oven), a Freedom induction cooktop, fridge/freezer, and microwave drawer all by Thermadore. &nbsp;Direct access to the covered patio and outdoor kitchen through a sliding glass door, an oversized quartz centre island with tons of room for preparing meals and seating for 4. LARGE WALK-IN PANTRY will allow you to select from the many small kitchen appliances and other accessories such as juicers, pressure cookers, pop corn maker, Soda Stream, Le Creuset and All Clad cookware, and more. &nbsp;A large selection of spices and other cooking necessities will help prevent trips to the store while making your fantastic meals. THE EXPANSIVE GREAT ROOM with 28 foot Fleetwood recessed doors lead out to the covered patio and seamlessly integrate the indoor and outdoor space. RETIRE TO THE MASTER BEDROOM with its scenic mountain top views to the South, and pool/spa and more mountains to the West.&nbsp; King bed with ultra high end Custom Comfort mattress and linens.&nbsp; Two day beds in spacious sitting area for some reading.&nbsp; 65’ Samsung HDTV flat screen with in ceiling speakers.&nbsp; Blinds, lighting, and TV control via remote/smartphone. THE SPA LIKE MASTER BATHROOM features dual vanities, a 10 ft long shower with dual rain showers above, and instant on steam with 2 benches to sit and relax while listening to the in-ceiling/shower sound.&nbsp; Or take a bath in the modern soaking tub while you watch a movie on the 40 inch flat screen.&nbsp; Start your morning with a walk outside to the private garden retreat where you can shower while enjoying the fresh scents of white roses, jasmine, and orange trees. EXTRA LARGE WALK IN CLOSET with seating and every woman’s dream vanity area. &nbsp;&nbsp; MEDIA ROOM features an 85’ 4k TV with 7 channel surround sound set against a walnut covered wall.&nbsp; Custom made designer couch and ottoman provide amazing comfort.&nbsp; Great soundproofing in media room allows you to enjoy the great sound system without disturbing other guests in the house. HOME OFFICE in case you want to get a little work done on your vacation.&nbsp; Sit in comfort in the Herman Miller – Eames Executive Soft Pad chair, and choose either the mountain vista views and infinity pool out the office door, or the lawns and bougainvillea out the sliding door to back yard.&nbsp; Your office visitors can relax in the Womb Chair and you can both enjoy the 55 inch Samsung flat screen, in ceiling stereo sound, and automated blinds and lighting.&nbsp; Printer, scanner, and basic office supplies available for use. HOME GYM because you want to look good out by the pool.&nbsp; Features a commercial grade Precor elliptical unit (the same as the most popular ones found in fitness clubs), weights, bench, stretching area, and other accessories.&nbsp; Professional massage table which can be set up for an in-house massage, with discounted rates from Zeel (Uber for massages).&nbsp; Workout to your favourite music with in-ceiling stereo sound, or watch TV on the 60’ 4k Curved Samsung TV complete with Apple TV.&nbsp; Gym has an ensuite full bathroom and shower, and opens up via a sliding door out to the backyard lawns and fruit trees. PRIVATE CASITA with separate entrance from the main home is perfect for guests.&nbsp; Complete with King bed, dual vanities and shower, large walk-in closet, 60’ HDTV and designer furnishings. Sliding door opens up onto the pool &amp; spa with amazing views to the West. 2ND GUEST ROOM in house with Queen bed and full ensuite. Views out to the fruit orchard. THE OUTDOOR LIVING SPACE is centered around the 48 foot infinity salt water pool and spa. Enjoy the shallow tanning shelf with two Ledge Lounger chaises and in water umbrella and table.&nbsp; On the pool deck, amazingly comfy bean bag chaises from Restoration Hardware.&nbsp; Enjoy the gas fire at night. &nbsp;On the 400 sq ft covered patio, you will enjoy a Vegas cabana style patio set from Royal Botania, and a large Richard Schultz 1966 dining table with 8 matching chairs.&nbsp; The entire patio perimeter is surrounded by misters to help keep you cool when needed.&nbsp; The outdoor kitchen is equip with a 42 inch Lynx Grill with infrared burner and rotisserie, plumbed sink, and a large built in bar center with ice chest…enjoy it all on a large cooking/dining island with 3 classic Bertoia chairs.&nbsp; Clean and modern landscaping, architectural landscape lighting, including the multi-color pool and spa LED lights, make for a breathtaking night time setting. FRUIT ORCHARD on the north east area of the property is young, but already bearing very nice fruits. Includes peaches, grapefruits, pomegranate, figs and a couple different varieties of lemons, limes, and oranges. Please note that these do not all produce at all times of year. SPECIAL SERVICES: In-house massage by Zeel. Book online or via the Zeel app and receive discounted rates with the annual membership attached to this property. In-house personal trainer with one of the top trainers from Next Level fitness. Preferred rates have been negotiated, but dependent upon duration and frequency. In-house private yoga sessions. Catering, event and wedding planning, and photography arrangements also possible with several of the Deserts finest (we did our own wedding here and have excellent referrals). &nbsp;
                      </div>
